/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[AUTOJOURNAL_ENTRYCHK]    Script Date: 06/26/2026 15:55:49 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER OFF
GO
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[AUTOJOURNAL_ENTRYCHK] AS DECLARE @ENTRYCODE AS NVARCHAR(20) DECLARE @ENTRYTYPE AS NVARCHAR(20) DECLARE @LGR_ID AS NVARCHAR(20) DECLARE @AMOUNT AS NVARCHAR(20) DECLARE @SQL AS NVARCHAR(4000) DECLARE @RETURN_ID NVARCHAR(10) declare @PARMDEFINITION nvarchar(500) declare @OUTVALUE as nvarchar(10) DECLARE @AMT AS FLOAT SET @SQL ="" SET @PARMDEFINITION = " @RETURN_ID NVARCHAR(10) OUTPUT" BEGIN IF EXISTS (SELECT * FROM sys.objects WHERE object_id = OBJECT_ID(N'[dbo].ENRTYCHK_TABLE') AND type in (N'U')) DROP TABLE ENRTYCHK_TABLE CREATE TABLE ENRTYCHK_TABLE(ENTRYCODE INT ,ENTRYTYPE NVARCHAR(20),LGR_ID INT ,AMOUNT FLOAT) END BEGIN SET @SQL =" DECLARE CUR_AUTOJOURNAL CURSOR FAST_FORWARD FOR SELECT VCODE,ENTRYTYPE,LGR_ID,(ISNULL(DRAMOUNT,0)+ISNULL(CRAMOUNT,0)) AS AMOUNT FROM AUTOJOURNAL AJ WHERE AJ.ENTRYTYPE NOT IN('T','JP','YP') AND LGR_ID NOT IN (7601,7600) " EXECUTE SP_EXECUTESQL @SQL OPEN CUR_AUTOJOURNAL FETCH NEXT FROM CUR_AUTOJOURNAL INTO @ENTRYCODE,@ENTRYTYPE,@LGR_ID,@AMOUNT WHILE @@FETCH_STATUS=0 BEGIN SET @OUTVALUE="" SET @SQL= "SELECT @RETURN_ID=ENTRYCODE FROM ADJMASTER AJ WHERE AJ.ENTRYCODE="+@ENTRYCODE+" AND AJ.TYPE='"+@ENTRYTYPE+"' AND AJ.LGR_ID="+@LGR_ID +" GROUP BY ENTRYCODE,TYPE,LGR_ID HAVING (SUM(ISNULL(DISCOUNT,0)+ISNULL(OTHERLESS,0))="+@AMOUNT+ " OR SUM(ISNULL(INTEREST,0))="+@AMOUNT+") " EXECUTE SP_EXECUTESQL @SQL, @PARMDEFINITION, @RETURN_ID = @OUTVALUE OUTPUT BEGIN IF @OUTVALUE="" OR @OUTVALUE IS NULL BEGIN SET @SQL= "SELECT @RETURN_ID=ENTRYCODE FROM PURADJMASTER AJ WHERE AJ.ENTRYCODE="+@ENTRYCODE+" AND AJ.TYPE='"+@ENTRYTYPE+"' AND AJ.LGR_ID="+@LGR_ID +" GROUP BY ENTRYCODE,TYPE,LGR_ID HAVING (SUM(ISNULL(DISCOUNT,0)+ISNULL(RD,0))="+@AMOUNT+ " OR SUM(ISNULL(INTEREST,0))="+@AMOUNT+") " EXECUTE SP_EXECUTESQL @SQL, @PARMDEFINITION, @RETURN_ID = @OUTVALUE OUTPUT IF @OUTVALUE="" OR @OUTVALUE IS NULL BEGIN SET @SQL=" INSERT INTO ENRTYCHK_TABLE VALUES("+@ENTRYCODE+",'"+@ENTRYTYPE +"',"+@LGR_ID+","+@AMOUNT+")" PRINT @SQL EXECUTE SP_EXECUTESQL @SQL END END END FETCH NEXT FROM CUR_AUTOJOURNAL INTO @ENTRYCODE,@ENTRYTYPE,@LGR_ID,@AMOUNT END CLOSE CUR_AUTOJOURNAL DEALLOCATE CUR_AUTOJOURNAL END
GO

/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[PRO_CHECK_DELETE_REFERENCE]    Script Date: 06/26/2026 15:55:50 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER OFF
GO
CREATE procedure [dbo].[PRO_CHECK_DELETE_REFERENCE] ( @ref_col as nvarchar(4000), @ref_col_val as nvarchar(20), @ref_table_name as nvarchar(500), @ref_exist as int output ) as declare @tableName as nvarchar(100) declare @ColName as nvarchar(100) declare @sql as nvarchar(2000) declare @return_id nvarchar(10) declare @outValue as nvarchar(10) declare @parmDefinition nvarchar(500) declare @tableId as nvarchar(500) declare @ref_table_id as nvarchar(500) Declare @curSQL as nvarchar(2000) Declare @TableSQL as nvarchar(4000) Declare @SQL1 as nvarchar(4000) begin set @sql = '' set @sql1 = '' SET @parmDefinition = N'@return_id nvarchar(10) OUTPUT' set @ref_exist = 0 set @sql = N'SELECT Id FROM SYSCOLUMNS WHERE name IN('+ @ref_col + ') and Id not in (select id from dbo.sysobjects where xtype not in (''v'') and [name] in (' + @ref_table_name + '))' set @curSQL = N'DECLARE ColCur CURSOR FAST_FORWARD FOR ' + @sql print @curSQL EXECUTE sp_executesql @curSQL Open colCur fetch next from colCur into @tableId WHILE @@FETCH_STATUS = 0 BEGIN if( @ref_exist = 1) begin break end print @ref_col print @tableId set @sql1=' select SO.[name] ,SC.[NAME] from dbo.sysobjects SO INNER JOIN SYSCOLUMNS SC ON SO.ID=SC.ID where SO.xtype not in (''v'') and SC.[NAME] IN('+@ref_col+') and SO.id ='+ @tableId set @TableSQL =N' DECLARE TableCur CURSOR FAST_FORWARD FOR '+ @sql1 print @TableSQL EXECUTE sp_executesql @TableSQL Open TableCur fetch next from TableCur into @tableName ,@ColName WHILE @@FETCH_STATUS = 0 BEGIN SELECT @sql = N'Select @return_id = ' + @ColName + ' from ' + @tableName + ' where ' + @ColName + ' = ' + @ref_col_val + '' EXECUTE sp_executesql @sql, @parmDefinition, @return_id = @outValue OUTPUT if(@outValue <> '' or @outValue <> NULL ) begin select @ref_exist = 1 print @ref_exist print @tableName break end else begin select @ref_exist = 0 print @ref_exist end Fetch next from TableCur into @tableName ,@ColName END CLOSE TableCur DEALLOCATE TableCur fetch next from colCur into @tableId end CLOSE colCur DEALLOCATE colCur end
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[PRO_CHANGE_YEAR] ( @newDb as nvarchar(50), @oldDb as nvarchar(50), @cmp_code as nvarchar(6) ) AS declare @sql as nvarchar(4000) begin set @sql = "" set @sql = "Insert into " + @newDb + "Item_Opening_Stock select * from "+ @oldDb + "Item_Opening_Stock A where A.cmp_code = " + @cmp_code + " and not exists (select " + @newDb + "Item_Opening_Stock .* from " + @newDb + "Item_Opening_Stock where " + @newDb + "Item_Opening_Stock.Item_Id = A.Item_Id and "+ @newDb + "Item_Opening_Stock.cmp_code = " + @cmp_code + ")" EXECUTE sp_executesql @sql set @sql = "" set @sql = A.cmp_ServiceTax_No," + @newDb + "Company_Master.cmp_Tds_No = A.cmp_Tds_No," + @newDb + "Company_Master.cmp_Pan_No = A.cmp_Pan_No," + @newDb + "Company_Master.cmp_Alias = A.cmp_Alias," + @newDb + "Company_Master.cmp_Inv_Hading = A.cmp_Inv_Hading," + @newDb + "Company_Master.cmp_Item_Hading = A.cmp_Item_Hading," + @newDb + "Company_Master.cmp_Specification = A.cmp_Specification," + @newDb + "Company_Master.cmp_Registration_No = A.cmp_Registration_No," + @newDb + "Company_Master.cmp_Jurisdiction = A.cmp_Jurisdiction," + @newDb + "Company_Master.cmp_InterestRate = A.cmp_InterestRate," + @newDb + "Company_Master.cmp_Contact_Person = A.cmp_Contact_Person," + @newDb + "Company_Master.cmp_Add1 = A.cmp_Add1," + @newDb + "Company_Master.cmp_Add2 = A.cmp_Add2," + @newDb + "Company_Master.cmp_City = A.cmp_City," + @newDb + "Company_Master.cmp_Pincode = A.cmp_Pincode," + @newDb + "Company_Master.cmp_State = A.cmp_State," + @newDb + "Company_Master.cmp_Phone1 = A.cmp_Phone1," + @newDb + "Company_Master.cmp_Phone2 = A.cmp_Phone2," + @newDb + "Company_Master.cmp_Mobile = A.cmp_Mobile," + @newDb + "Company_Master.cmp_Fax = A.cmp_Fax," + @newDb + "Company_Master.cmp_Email = A.cmp_Email," + @newDb + "Company_Master.cmp_Web = A.cmp_Web," + @newDb + "Company_Master.cmp_Fc_Add1 = A.cmp_Fc_Add1," + @newDb + "Company_Master.cmp_Fc_Add2 = A.cmp_Fc_Add2," + @newDb + "Company_Master.cmp_Fc_City = A.cmp_Fc_City," + @newDb + "Company_Master.cmp_Fc_Pincode = A.cmp_Fc_Pincode," + @newDb + "Company_Master.cmp_Fc_State = A.cmp_Fc_State," + @newDb + "Company_Master.cmp_Round_Off = A.cmp_Round_Off From " + @newDb + "Company_Master inner join " + @oldDb + "Company_Master A on " + @newDb + "Company_Master.cmp_code = A.cmp_code where " + @newDb + "Company_Master.cmp_code = " + @cmp_code + " and A.cmp_code = " + @cmp_code EXECUTE sp_executesql @sql set @sql = "" set @sql = "Insert into " + @newDb + "Company_Master select * from "+ @oldDb + "Company_Master A where A.cmp_code = " + @cmp_code + " and not exists (select " + @newDb + "Company_Master .* from " + @newDb + "Company_Master where " + @newDb + "Company_Master.cmp_code = A.cmp_code and "+ @newDb + "Company_Master.cmp_code = " + @cmp_code + ")" EXECUTE sp_executesql @sql end

/****** Object:  View [dbo].[OpeningStock_Ledger]    Script Date: 06/26/2026 15:55:51 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
create view [dbo].[OpeningStock_Ledger] as SELECT TM.TRAN_MASTER_ID LEDGERCODE,CASE WHEN TM.TRAN_DRCR = 'D' THEN TM.TRAN_AMOUNT ELSE 0 END AS OPDRAMT, CASE WHEN TM.TRAN_DRCR = 'C' THEN TM.TRAN_AMOUNT ELSE 0 END AS OPCRAMT, TM.CMP_CODE,TM.TRAN_DATE AS VDATE,CM.CITY_NAME LCITY FROM TRAN_MASTER TM INNER JOIN LEDGER_MASTER LM ON TM.TRAN_MASTER_ID=LM.LGR_ID LEFT OUTER JOIN CITY_MASTER CM ON LM.CITY_ID=CM.CITY_ID INNER JOIN TRAN_DETAIL TD ON TM.TRAN_ID=TD.TRAN_ID AND TM.TRAN_TYPE=TD.TRAN_TYPE WHERE TM.CMP_CODE=1 AND TM.TRAN_TYPE <> 'J' AND LM.LGR_ID=14199 AND TM.TRAN_DATE<'01/Apr/2019' UNION ALL SELECT TD.TRAN_DETAIL_ID, CASE WHEN TD.TRAN_DRCR = 'D' THEN TD.TRAN_AMOUNT ELSE 0 END AS DEBITAMOUNT, CASE WHEN TD.TRAN_DRCR = 'C' THEN TD.TRAN_AMOUNT ELSE 0 END AS CREDITAMOUNT, TD.CMP_CODE,TM.TRAN_DATE AS VDATE,CM.CITY_NAME AS CITY FROM TRAN_MASTER TM INNER JOIN TRAN_DETAIL TD ON TM.TRAN_ID=TD.TRAN_ID AND TM.TRAN_TYPE=TD.TRAN_TYPE INNER JOIN LEDGER_MASTER LM ON TD.TRAN_DETAIL_ID=LM.LGR_ID LEFT OUTER JOIN CITY_MASTER CM ON LM.CITY_ID=CM.CITY_ID WHERE TM.CMP_CODE=1 AND LM.LGR_ID=14199 AND TM.TRAN_DATE<'01/Apr/2019' UNION ALL SELECT AJ.LGR_ID,CASE WHEN ISNULL(AJ.DRAMOUNT, 0) <> 0 THEN AJ.DRAMOUNT ELSE 0 END AS DEBITAMOUNT, CASE WHEN ISNULL(AJ.CRAMOUNT, 0) <> 0 THEN AJ.CRAMOUNT ELSE 0 END AS CREDITAMOUNT, AJ.CMP_CODE,AJ.VDATE,CM.CITY_NAME AS CITY FROM AUTOJOURNAL AJ INNER JOIN LEDGER_MASTER LM ON AJ.LGR_ID=LM.LGR_ID INNER JOIN CITY_MASTER CM ON LM.CITY_ID=CM.CITY_ID WHERE AJ.CMP_CODE=1 AND LM.LGR_ID=14199 AND AJ.VDATE<'01/Apr/2019' UNION ALL SELECT 14199 LEDGERCODE,CASE WHEN LD.LGR_OP_DRCR = 'D' THEN LD.LGR_OP_BAL WHEN LD.LGR_OP_DRCR = '' THEN LD.LGR_OP_BAL ELSE 0 END AS OPDRAMT, CASE WHEN LD.LGR_OP_DRCR = 'C' THEN LD.LGR_OP_BAL WHEN LD.LGR_OP_BAL = 0 THEN LD.LGR_OP_BAL ELSE 0 END AS OPCRAMT, LD.CMP_CODE,'01/Apr/2019' AS VDATE,CM.CITY_NAME LCITY FROM LEDGER_DETAIL LD INNER JOIN LEDGER_MASTER LM ON LD.LGR_ID=LM.LGR_ID LEFT OUTER JOIN CITY_MASTER CM ON LM.CITY_ID=CM.CITY_ID WHERE LD.CMP_CODE=1 AND LM.LGR_ID=14199
GO
/****** Object:  View [dbo].[OpeningStock]    Script Date: 06/26/2026 15:55:51 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
create view [dbo].[OpeningStock] as SELECT TM.tran_Master_id LedgerCode,CASE WHEN TM.Tran_drcr = 'D' THEN TM.Tran_amount ELSE 0 END AS OpDrAmt,CASE WHEN TM.Tran_drcr = 'C' THEN TM.Tran_amount  ELSE 0 END AS OpCrAmt,  TM.cmp_Code,CM.City_name LCity,TM.Tran_Date as VDate  FROM Tran_Master TM   INNER JOIN TRAN_DETAIL TD ON TM.TRAN_ID=TD.TRAN_ID AND TM.TRAN_TYPE=TD.TRAN_TYPE   INNER JOIN Ledger_Master LM ON TM.tran_Master_id=LM.lgr_id  LEFT OUTER JOIN City_Master CM ON LM.City_id=CM.City_id   WHERE TM.Tran_Type <> 'J'  and tm.tran_type not in ('')  UNION ALL    SELECT TD.Tran_Detail_id, CASE WHEN TD.Tran_drcr = 'D' THEN TD.Tran_amount ELSE 0 END AS Debitamount,   CASE WHEN TD.Tran_drcr = 'C' THEN TD.Tran_amount  ELSE 0 END AS Creditamount, TD.cmp_Code,CM.City_Name as CITY ,TM.Tran_Date as VDate  FROM Tran_Master TM   INNER JOIN Tran_Detail TD ON TM.Tran_ID=TD.Tran_ID AND TM.Tran_Type=TD.Tran_Type   INNER JOIN Ledger_Master LM ON TD.Tran_Detail_id=LM.Lgr_Id   LEFT OUTER JOIN City_Master CM ON LM.City_ID=CM.City_ID  where tm.tran_type not in ('')  UNION ALL     SELECT AJ.Lgr_ID,CASE WHEN ISNULL(AJ.drAmount, 0) <> 0 THEN AJ.DrAmount ELSE 0 END AS Debitamount,   CASE WHEN ISNULL(AJ.CrAmount, 0) <> 0 THEN AJ.CrAmount ELSE 0 END   AS Creditamount, AJ.cmp_code,CM.City_Name as CITY,AJ.Vdate  FROM AutoJournal AJ   INNER JOIN Ledger_Master LM ON AJ.Lgr_ID=LM.Lgr_ID   INNER JOIN City_Master CM ON LM.City_ID=CM.City_ID   UNION ALL    SELECT LD.Lgr_ID, CASE WHEN Lgr_op_drcr = 'D' THEN Lgr_op_bal WHEN Lgr_op_drcr = '' THEN Lgr_op_bal ELSE 0 END AS DebitAmount,  CASE WHEN Lgr_op_drcr = 'C' THEN Lgr_op_bal WHEN Lgr_op_drcr = '' THEN Lgr_op_bal ELSE 0 END AS CreditAmount, LD.Cmp_Code,CM.City_Name,'01/Jan/1900' AS VDATE   FROM Ledger_Detail LD   INNER JOIN Ledger_Master LM ON LD.Lgr_ID=LM.Lgr_ID    LEFT OUTER JOIN City_Master CM ON LM.City_Id=CM.City_ID
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[PRO_INVOICE_DETAILS]    Script Date: 06/26/2026 15:55:51 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER OFF
GO
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[PRO_INVOICE_DETAILS] ( @Sal_Inv_Id as numeric, @cmp_code as int ) AS begin select si.*,lm.Lgr_Name as Party_Name,tm.Transport_Name,cm.City_Name as Station_Name, alm.Lgr_Name as Agent_Name from Sales_Invoice si left outer join Ledger_Master lm on si.Lgr_Id = lm.Lgr_Id left outer join Transport_Master tm on si.Transport_Id = tm.Transport_Id left outer join city_Master cm on si.Station_Id = cm.city_Id left outer join Ledger_Master alm on si.Agent_Id = alm.Lgr_Id where si.Sal_Inv_Id = @Sal_Inv_Id and si.cmp_code = @cmp_code end RETURN
GO

NVARCHAR(200), @LGR_POST AS NVARCHAR(150), @CUST_GRP_ID AS INT, @SUPP_GRP_ID AS INT, @SALESMANID AS INT, @CATEGORY_ID AS INT, @GEN_GRP_ID AS INT, @COURIERMASTER_ID AS INT, @LGR_COMMITION AS FLOAT, NVARCHAR(50), @LGR_PANO AS NVARCHAR(18), @LGR_CSTNO AS NVARCHAR(18), @LGR_TDSNO AS NVARCHAR(18), @LGR_STNO AS NVARCHAR(18), @LGR_TYPE AS NVARCHAR(1), @LGR_STATION_ID AS INT, @CMP_CODE AS INT, @GRP_ID AS INT, @AGENT_ID AS NVARCHAR(10), @TRANSPORT_ID AS INT, @LGR_OP_BAL AS FLOAT, @LGR_OP_DRCR AS NVARCHAR(1), @LGR_CL_BAL AS FLOAT, @LGR_CL_DRCR AS NVARCHAR(1), @BEDIT AS INT, @TDSAPP AS CHAR(1), @DEDUCTEE_CODE AS INT, @TDSNATURE_CODE AS INT, @TDSNATUREACID AS NVARCHAR(150), @TDSONBILL AS CHAR(1), @TDSALLBILL AS CHAR(1), @TDSRATE AS FLOAT , @CITY_PINCODE AS INT, @LGR_STOP NVARCHAR(10), @INV_STOP NVARCHAR(10), @BF1STHALF FLOAT, @AF1STHALF FLOAT, @ACCOUNT_ID INT, @OPNG_DEP_PER FLOAT, @ADD_DATE NVARCHAR(50), @EDIT_DATE NVARCHAR(50), @USERID INT, @PAYEE_ID INT, @TDS_ID INT, @TDS_B4LR_CERTI FLOAT, @DATE_LRCERTI SMALLDATETIME, @TDS_PER_ALRCERTI_EXC FLOAT, @TDS_LMT_LRCERTI FLOAT, @INSURED NVARCHAR(10), @LGR_IFSCCODE NVARCHAR(50), @LGR_BANKACCNO NVARCHAR(50), @STAMPGRP_ID NVARCHAR(50), @TRANS_PER FLOAT, @LGR_SPRD FLOAT, @LGR_SPSWEET FLOAT, @LGR_GROSSDAYS INT, @LGR_DISCOUNT FLOAT, @LGR_CR_PERIOD_DAY AS INT, @LGR_SY_SPRD FLOAT, @LGR_SY_SPSWEET FLOAT, @LGR_SY_DISCOUNT FLOAT, @LGR_SY_INTERESTRATE FLOAT, @LGR_SY_CRDAYS AS INT, @LGR_TERMS NVARCHAR(10), @LGR_PASSWORD NVARCHAR(100), @JOB_TYPE NVARCHAR(100), @PAYMENTDAYS INT, @BALANCE_LIMIT FLOAT, @GSTINNO NVARCHAR(15), @ADHARNO NVARCHAR(20), @Register_Dealer_Type NVARCHAR(50), @Supply_Type NVARCHAR(50), @Gst_Supply_Type NVARCHAR(50), @IECODE NVARCHAR(20), @BANKTYPE NVARCHAR(100), @MSME_Code AS NVARCHAR(50),@MSME_Type AS NVARCHAR(50), @MSME_Category As Nvarchar(50) ) AS DECLARE @CMP_ID AS INT DECLARE @OP_CRDR AS NVARCHAR(1) DECLARE @CL_BAL AS FLOAT DECLARE @CL_CRDR AS NVARCHAR(1) DECLARE @TOTAL_CR_BAL AS FLOAT DECLARE @TOTAL_DR_BAL AS FLOAT BEGIN IF(@BEDIT = 0) BEGIN INSERT INTO ACC_MASTER.DBO.LEDGER_MASTER(LGR_ID, LGR_NAME,CITY_ID) VALUES(@LGR_ID, @LGR_NAME,@CITY_ID) INSERT INTO LEDGER_MASTER(LGR_ID, LGR_NAME,LGR_ALIAS,LGR_PRINTNAME,LGR_BANK,LGR_BRANCH,LGR_POST, CUST_GRP_ID, SUPP_GRP_ID, CATEGORY_ID, GEN_GRP_ID,COURIERMASTER_ID ,SALESMAN_ID, LGR_COMMITION, LGR_INTERESTRATE, LGR_CR_PERIOD_DAY, LGR_CR_LIMIT, LGR_ADD1, LGR_ADD2,LGR_ADD3,CITY_ID,STATE_ID, LGR_PHONE1, LGR_PHONE2, LGR_MOBILE, LGR_FAX, LGR_EMAIL, LGR_WEBSITE, LGR_CONT_PERSON, LGR_PANO, LGR_CSTNO,LGR_STNO, LGR_TDSNO, LGR_TYPE, LGR_STATION_ID,TDSAPP,DEDUCTEE_CODE,TDSNATURE_CODE, TDSNATUREACID,LGR_DISTRICT ,CITY_PINCODE, LGR_STOP,INV_STOP,BF1STHALF ,AF1STHALF,OPNG_DEP_PER , ADD_DATE, EDIT_DATE ,USERID,INSURED,LGR_IFSCCODE,LGR_BANKACCNO, STAMPGRP_ID,TRANS_PER,LGR_SY_INTERESTRATE,LGR_SY_CRDAYS,LGR_PASSWORD,JOB_TYPE,PAYMENTDAYS,GSTINNO,ADHARNO,Register_Dealer_Type,Supply_Type,Gst_Supply_Type,IECODE,BANKTYPE,MSME_Code,MSME_Type,MSME_Category) VALUES(@LGR_ID, @LGR_NAME, @LGR_ALIAS,@LGR_PRINTNAME ,@LGR_BANK,@LGR_BRANCH,@LGR_POST,@CUST_GRP_ID, @SUPP_GRP_ID, @CATEGORY_ID, @GEN_GRP_ID,@COURIERMASTER_ID,@SALESMANID,@LGR_COMMITION, @LGR_INTERESTRATE, @LGR_CR_PERIOD_DAY, @LGR_CR_LIMIT, @LGR_ADD1, @LGR_ADD2,@LGR_ADD3,@CITY_ID, @STATE_ID, @LGR_PHONE1, @LGR_PHONE2, @LGR_MOBILE, @LGR_FAX, @LGR_EMAIL, @LGR_WEBSITE, @LGR_CONT_PERSON, @LGR_PANO, @LGR_CSTNO, @LGR_STNO,@LGR_TDSNO,@LGR_TYPE, @LGR_STATION_ID, @TDSAPP,@DEDUCTEE_CODE,@TDSNATURE_CODE,@TDSNATUREACID, @LGR_DISTRICT,@CITY_PINCODE,@LGR_STOP,@INV_STOP,@BF1STHALF ,@AF1STHALF,@OPNG_DEP_PER,@ADD_DATE,@EDIT_DATE,@USERID, @INSURED,@LGR_IFSCCODE, @LGR_BANKACCNO,@STAMPGRP_ID,@TRANS_PER,@LGR_SY_INTERESTRATE,@LGR_SY_CRDAYS, @LGR_PASSWORD,@JOB_TYPE,@PAYMENTDAYS,@GSTINNO ,@ADHARNO ,@Register_Dealer_Type,@Supply_Type,@Gst_Supply_Type,@IECODE,@BANKTYPE,@MSME_Code,@MSME_Type,@MSME_Category) INSERT INTO LEDGER_DETAIL(LGR_ID, CMP_CODE, GRP_ID, AGENT_ID, TRANSPORT_ID, LGR_OP_BAL, LGR_OP_DRCR, LGR_CL_BAL, LGR_CL_DRCR,LGR_TOTAL_CR_BAL, LGR_TOTAL_DR_BAL,ACCOUNT_ID,PAYEE_ID,TDS_ID,TDSONBILL,TDSRATE,TDS_B4LR_CERTI, DATE_LRCERTI,TDS_PER_ALRCERTI_EXC,TDS_LMT_LRCERTI,TDSALLBILL,LGR_SPRD,LGR_SPSWEET,LGR_GROSSDAYS,LGR_DISCOUNT, LGR_SY_SPRD,LGR_SY_SPSWEET,LGR_SY_DISCOUNT,LGR_TERMS,BALANCE_LIMIT) VALUES(@LGR_ID, @CMP_CODE, @GRP_ID, @AGENT_ID, @TRANSPORT_ID, @LGR_OP_BAL, @LGR_OP_DRCR, @LGR_CL_BAL, @LGR_CL_DRCR,0,0,@ACCOUNT_ID,@PAYEE_ID,@TDS_ID, @TDSONBILL,@TDSRATE,@TDS_B4LR_CERTI,@DATE_LRCERTI, @TDS_PER_ALRCERTI_EXC,@TDS_LMT_LRCERTI,@TDSALLBILL, @LGR_SPRD,@LGR_SPSWEET,@LGR_GROSSDAYS,@LGR_DISCOUNT, @LGR_SY_SPRD,@LGR_SY_SPSWEET,@LGR_SY_DISCOUNT,@LGR_TERMS,@BALANCE_LIMIT) DECLARE CMPCUR CURSOR FAST_FORWARD FOR SELECT CMP_CODE FROM COMPANY_MASTER WHERE CMP_CODE <> @CMP_CODE OPEN CMPCUR FETCH NEXT FROM CMPCUR INTO @CMP_ID WHILE @@FETCH_STATUS = 0 BEGIN INSERT INTO LEDGER_DETAIL(LGR_ID, CMP_CODE, GRP_ID, AGENT_ID, TRANSPORT_ID, LGR_OP_BAL, LGR_OP_DRCR, LGR_CL_BAL, LGR_CL_DRCR,LGR_TOTAL_CR_BAL, LGR_TOTAL_DR_BAL,ACCOUNT_ID,PAYEE_ID,TDS_ID, TDSONBILL,TDSRATE, TDS_B4LR_CERTI,DATE_LRCERTI,TDS_PER_ALRCERTI_EXC,TDS_LMT_LRCERTI,TDSALLBILL,LGR_SPRD,LGR_SPSWEET,LGR_GROSSDAYS, LGR_DISCOUNT,LGR_SY_SPRD,LGR_SY_SPSWEET,LGR_SY_DISCOUNT,LGR_TERMS,BALANCE_LIMIT) VALUES(@LGR_ID, @CMP_ID, @GRP_ID, @AGENT_ID, @TRANSPORT_ID, 0, "C", 0, "C",0,0,@ACCOUNT_ID, @PAYEE_ID,@TDS_ID, @TDSONBILL,@TDSRATE,@TDS_B4LR_CERTI,@DATE_LRCERTI,@TDS_PER_ALRCERTI_EXC, @TDS_LMT_LRCERTI,@TDSALLBILL,0,0,0,0,0, 0,0,0,@BALANCE_LIMIT) FETCH NEXT FROM CMPCUR INTO @CMP_ID END CLOSE CMPCUR DEALLOCATE CMPCUR END ELSE BEGIN UPDATE ACC_MASTER.DBO.LEDGER_MASTER SET LGR_NAME = @LGR_NAME,CITY_ID = @CITY_ID WHERE LGR_ID = @LGR_ID UPDATE LEDGER_MASTER SET LGR_NAME = @LGR_NAME, LGR_ALIAS = @LGR_ALIAS, LGR_PRINTNAME=@LGR_PRINTNAME, LGR_BANK=@LGR_BANK,LGR_BRANCH=@LGR_BRANCH,LGR_POST=@LGR_POST, CUST_GRP_ID = @CUST_GRP_ID, SUPP_GRP_ID = @SUPP_GRP_ID, CATEGORY_ID = @CATEGORY_ID, GEN_GRP_ID = @GEN_GRP_ID, COURIERMASTER_ID=@COURIERMASTER_ID , LGR_COMMITION = @LGR_COMMITION, LGR_INTERESTRATE = @LGR_INTERESTRATE, LGR_CR_PERIOD_DAY = @LGR_CR_PERIOD_DAY, LGR_CR_LIMIT = @LGR_CR_LIMIT, LGR_ADD1 = @LGR_ADD1, LGR_ADD2 = @LGR_ADD2,LGR_ADD3 = @LGR_ADD3, CITY_ID = @CITY_ID, STATE_ID = @STATE_ID, LGR_PHONE1 = @LGR_PHONE1, LGR_PHONE2 = @LGR_PHONE2, LGR_MOBILE = @LGR_MOBILE, LGR_FAX = @LGR_FAX, LGR_EMAIL = @LGR_EMAIL, LGR_WEBSITE = @LGR_WEBSITE, LGR_CONT_PERSON = @LGR_CONT_PERSON, LGR_PANO = @LGR_PANO, LGR_CSTNO = @LGR_CSTNO, LGR_STNO = @LGR_STNO, LGR_TDSNO=@LGR_TDSNO, LGR_TYPE = @LGR_TYPE, LGR_STATION_ID = @LGR_STATION_ID, TDSAPP=@TDSAPP, DEDUCTEE_CODE=@DEDUCTEE_CODE, TDSNATURE_CODE=@TDSNATURE_CODE, TDSNATUREACID=@TDSNATUREACID, SALESMAN_ID=@SALESMANID, LGR_DISTRICT=@LGR_DISTRICT,CITY_PINCODE=@CITY_PINCODE ,LGR_STOP =@LGR_STOP , INV_STOP=@INV_STOP,BF1STHALF =@BF1STHALF , AF1STHALF =@AF1STHALF ,OPNG_DEP_PER=@OPNG_DEP_PER,ADD_DATE=@ADD_DATE, EDIT_DATE=@EDIT_DATE,USERID=@USERID, INSURED=@INSURED,LGR_IFSCCODE = @LGR_IFSCCODE, LGR_BANKACCNO = @LGR_BANKACCNO,STAMPGRP_ID = @STAMPGRP_ID, TRANS_PER = @TRANS_PER, LGR_SY_INTERESTRATE = @LGR_SY_INTERESTRATE,LGR_SY_CRDAYS = @LGR_SY_CRDAYS, LGR_PASSWORD = @LGR_PASSWORD,JOB_TYPE = @JOB_TYPE,PAYMENTDAYS=@PAYMENTDAYS,GSTINNO =@GSTINNO ,ADHARNO = @ADHARNO ,Register_Dealer_Type = @Register_Dealer_Type ,Supply_Type = @Supply_Type ,Gst_Supply_Type = @Gst_Supply_Type ,IECODE = @IECODE,BANKTYPE = @BANKTYPE,MSME_Code = @MSME_Code,MSME_Type=@MSME_Type,MSME_Category = @MSME_Category WHERE LGR_ID = @LGR_ID SELECT @TOTAL_CR_BAL = LGR_TOTAL_CR_BAL, @TOTAL_DR_BAL = LGR_TOTAL_DR_BAL FROM LEDGER_DETAIL WHERE LGR_ID = @LGR_ID AND CMP_CODE = @CMP_CODE IF (@LGR_OP_DRCR = "C") BEGIN SET @CL_BAL = (@LGR_OP_BAL + @TOTAL_CR_BAL) - @TOTAL_DR_BAL IF(@CL_BAL < 0) BEGIN SET @CL_BAL = ABS(@CL_BAL) SET @CL_CRDR = "D" END ELSE BEGIN SET @CL_CRDR = "C" END END ELSE BEGIN SET @CL_BAL = (@LGR_OP_BAL + @TOTAL_DR_BAL) - @TOTAL_CR_BAL IF(@CL_BAL < 0) BEGIN SET @CL_BAL = ABS(@CL_BAL) SET @CL_CRDR = "C" END ELSE BEGIN SET @CL_CRDR = "D" END END UPDATE LEDGER_DETAIL SET AGENT_ID = @AGENT_ID,GRP_ID=@GRP_ID, TRANSPORT_ID = @TRANSPORT_ID, LGR_OP_BAL = @LGR_OP_BAL, LGR_OP_DRCR = @LGR_OP_DRCR, LGR_CL_BAL = @CL_BAL, LGR_CL_DRCR = @CL_CRDR, ACCOUNT_ID=@ACCOUNT_ID,PAYEE_ID=@PAYEE_ID, TDS_ID=@TDS_ID,TDSONBILL=@TDSONBILL,TDSRATE=@TDSRATE, TDS_B4LR_CERTI=@TDS_B4LR_CERTI, DATE_LRCERTI=@DATE_LRCERTI,TDS_PER_ALRCERTI_EXC=@TDS_PER_ALRCERTI_EXC, TDS_LMT_LRCERTI=@TDS_LMT_LRCERTI, TDSALLBILL=@TDSALLBILL, LGR_SPRD=@LGR_SPRD, LGR_SPSWEET=@LGR_SPSWEET, LGR_GROSSDAYS=@LGR_GROSSDAYS, LGR_DISCOUNT=@LGR_DISCOUNT, LGR_SY_SPRD=@LGR_SY_SPRD, LGR_SY_SPSWEET=@LGR_SY_SPSWEET, LGR_SY_DISCOUNT=@LGR_SY_DISCOUNT, LGR_TERMS=@LGR_TERMS,BALANCE_LIMIT =@BALANCE_LIMIT WHERE LGR_ID = @LGR_ID AND CMP_CODE = @CMP_CODE END END

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[PRO_INSERT_ITEM_MASTER] ( @ITEM_ID AS INT, @ITEM_NAME AS NVARCHAR(100), @UNIT_ID AS INT, @ITEM_GRP_ID AS INT, @ITEM_TYPE AS NVARCHAR(10), @ITEM_CONVERSION AS FLOAT, @ITEM_OP_STOCK AS FLOAT, @ITEM_CL_STOCK AS FLOAT, @ITEM_IN_QTY AS FLOAT, @ITEM_OUT_QTY AS FLOAT, @CMP_CODE AS INT, @ITEM_CUT AS FLOAT, @SAL_RATE AS FLOAT, @PUR_RATE AS FLOAT, @SNET_SAL_RATE AS FLOAT, @RATE_PER AS NVARCHAR(10), @ITEM_READS AS FLOAT, @ITEM_PEAK AS FLOAT, @ITEM_GWIDTH AS FLOAT, @ITEM_GWEIGHT AS FLOAT, @ITEM_DWEIGHT AS FLOAT, @ITEM_GOODS_TYPE AS NVARCHAR(50), @ITEM_TYPE_ID AS INT, @ITEM_WEIGHT AS FLOAT, @ITEM_OP_THAN AS INT, @BEDIT AS BIT, @ADD_DATE SMALLDATETIME, @EDIT_DATE AS SMALLDATETIME, @USERID AS INT, @SCHEME_PER AS FLOAT, @LOT_ID AS INT, @ORDERPCS_BALES AS INT, @PACKINGSTYLE_ID AS INT, @VATCAT_ID AS INT, @ITEM_MIN_QTY AS FLOAT, @ITEM_STOP NVARCHAR(10), @NICK_NAME AS NVARCHAR(200), @COLOR_PERS AS FLOAT, @HSN_ID as nvarchar(10), @CGST_PER AS FLOAT, @SGST_PER AS FLOAT, @IGST_PER AS FLOAT ) AS DECLARE @CMP_ID AS INT BEGIN IF(@BEDIT = 0) BEGIN INSERT INTO ACC_MASTER.DBO.ITEM_MASTER(ITEM_ID, ITEM_NAME,ITEM_CUT) VALUES(@ITEM_ID, @ITEM_NAME,@ITEM_CUT) INSERT INTO ITEM_MASTER(ITEM_ID, ITEM_NAME, UNIT_ID, ITEM_GRP_ID, ITEM_TYPE, ITEM_CONVERSION,ITEM_CUT,RATE_PER, ITEM_READS,ITEM_PEAK,ITEM_GWIDTH,ITEM_GWEIGHT, ITEM_DWEIGHT,ITEM_GOODS_TYPE,ITEM_TYPE_ID,ITEM_WEIGHT,ADD_DATE, EDIT_DATE,USERID, SCHEME_PER,LOT_ID,ORDERPCS_BALES,PACKINGSTYLE_ID,VATCAT_ID,ITEM_STOP,NICK_NAME,COLOR_PERS,HSN_ID,CGST_PER,SGST_PER,IGST_PER) VALUES(@ITEM_ID, @ITEM_NAME,@UNIT_ID,@ITEM_GRP_ID, @ITEM_TYPE, @ITEM_CONVERSION, @ITEM_CUT,@RATE_PER, @ITEM_READS,@ITEM_PEAK,@ITEM_GWIDTH,@ITEM_GWEIGHT,@ITEM_DWEIGHT, @ITEM_GOODS_TYPE,@ITEM_TYPE_ID, @ITEM_WEIGHT,@ADD_DATE,@EDIT_DATE,@USERID,@SCHEME_PER,@LOT_ID,@ORDERPCS_BALES,@PACKINGSTYLE_ID, @VATCAT_ID,@ITEM_STOP,@NICK_NAME,@COLOR_PERS,@HSN_ID,@CGST_PER,@SGST_PER,@IGST_PER) INSERT INTO ITEM_OPENING_STOCK(ITEM_ID, CMP_CODE, ITEM_OP_STOCK, ITEM_CL_STOCK, ITEM_IN_QTY, ITEM_OUT_QTY,SAL_RATE, PUR_RATE,SNET_SAL_RATE,ITEM_OP_THAN,ITEM_MIN_QTY) VALUES(@ITEM_ID,@CMP_CODE, @ITEM_OP_STOCK, @ITEM_CL_STOCK, @ITEM_IN_QTY, @ITEM_OUT_QTY,@SAL_RATE,@PUR_RATE, @SNET_SAL_RATE,@ITEM_OP_THAN,@ITEM_MIN_QTY) DECLARE CMPCUR CURSOR FAST_FORWARD FOR SELECT CMP_CODE FROM COMPANY_MASTER WHERE CMP_CODE <> @CMP_CODE OPEN CMPCUR FETCH NEXT FROM CMPCUR INTO @CMP_ID WHILE @@FETCH_STATUS = 0 BEGIN INSERT INTO ITEM_OPENING_STOCK(ITEM_ID, CMP_CODE, ITEM_OP_STOCK, ITEM_CL_STOCK, ITEM_IN_QTY, ITEM_OUT_QTY,SAL_RATE, PUR_RATE,SNET_SAL_RATE,ITEM_OP_THAN) VALUES(@ITEM_ID,@CMP_ID, 0,0, 0, 0, @SAL_RATE,@PUR_RATE,@SNET_SAL_RATE,0) FETCH NEXT FROM CMPCUR INTO @CMP_ID END CLOSE CMPCUR DEALLOCATE CMPCUR END ELSE BEGIN UPDATE ACC_MASTER.DBO.ITEM_MASTER SET ITEM_NAME = @ITEM_NAME,ITEM_CUT = @ITEM_CUT WHERE ITEM_ID = @ITEM_ID UPDATE ITEM_MASTER SET ITEM_NAME = @ITEM_NAME, UNIT_ID = @UNIT_ID, ITEM_GRP_ID = @ITEM_GRP_ID, ITEM_TYPE = @ITEM_TYPE, ITEM_CONVERSION = @ITEM_CONVERSION, ITEM_CUT=@ITEM_CUT ,RATE_PER=@RATE_PER, ITEM_READS=@ITEM_READS, ITEM_PEAK=@ITEM_PEAK, ITEM_GWIDTH=@ITEM_GWIDTH, ITEM_GWEIGHT=@ITEM_GWEIGHT, ITEM_DWEIGHT=@ITEM_DWEIGHT, ITEM_GOODS_TYPE=@ITEM_GOODS_TYPE, ITEM_TYPE_ID=@ITEM_TYPE_ID , ITEM_WEIGHT=@ITEM_WEIGHT,ADD_DATE=@ADD_DATE, EDIT_DATE=@EDIT_DATE,USERID=@USERID, SCHEME_PER=@SCHEME_PER,LOT_ID=@LOT_ID, ORDERPCS_BALES=@ORDERPCS_BALES,PACKINGSTYLE_ID = @PACKINGSTYLE_ID, VATCAT_ID = @VATCAT_ID,ITEM_STOP=@ITEM_STOP, NICK_NAME =@NICK_NAME,COLOR_PERS=@COLOR_PERS,HSN_ID=@HSN_ID, CGST_PER=@CGST_PER,SGST_PER=@SGST_PER,IGST_PER=@IGST_PER WHERE ITEM_ID = @ITEM_ID UPDATE ITEM_OPENING_STOCK SET ITEM_OP_STOCK = @ITEM_OP_STOCK, ITEM_CL_STOCK = @ITEM_CL_STOCK, ITEM_IN_QTY = @ITEM_IN_QTY, ITEM_OUT_QTY = @ITEM_OUT_QTY ,SAL_RATE=@SAL_RATE,PUR_RATE=@PUR_RATE, SNET_SAL_RATE=@SNET_SAL_RATE, ITEM_OP_THAN=@ITEM_OP_THAN,ITEM_MIN_QTY = @ITEM_MIN_QTY WHERE ITEM_ID = @ITEM_ID AND CMP_CODE = @CMP_CODE END END

GRP_NAME) VALUES(11,"Loans(Liabilities)") INSERT INTO ACC_MASTER.DBO.GROUP_MASTER(GRP_ID, GRP_NAME) VALUES(12,"Profit And Loss") INSERT INTO ACC_MASTER.DBO.GROUP_MASTER(GRP_ID, GRP_NAME) VALUES(13,"Capital") INSERT INTO ACC_MASTER.DBO.GROUP_MASTER(GRP_ID, GRP_NAME) VALUES(14,"Suspense Account") INSERT INTO ACC_MASTER.DBO.GROUP_MASTER(GRP_ID, GRP_NAME) VALUES(15,"Bank") INSERT INTO ACC_MASTER.DBO.GROUP_MASTER(GRP_ID, GRP_NAME) VALUES(20,"Provisions/Expense Payable") INSERT INTO ACC_MASTER.DBO.GROUP_MASTER(GRP_ID, GRP_NAME) VALUES(21,"Reserves And Surplus") INSERT INTO ACC_MASTER.DBO.GROUP_MASTER(GRP_ID, GRP_NAME) VALUES(22,"Secured Loans") INSERT INTO ACC_MASTER.DBO.GROUP_MASTER(GRP_ID, GRP_NAME) VALUES(23,"Security And Deposits") INSERT INTO ACC_MASTER.DBO.GROUP_MASTER(GRP_ID, GRP_NAME) VALUES(24,"Stock In Hand") INSERT INTO ACC_MASTER.DBO.GROUP_MASTER(GRP_ID, GRP_NAME) VALUES(25,"Sundry Creditors") INSERT INTO ACC_MASTER.DBO.GROUP_MASTER(GRP_ID, GRP_NAME) VALUES(26,"Sundry Debtors") INSERT INTO ACC_MASTER.DBO.GROUP_MASTER(GRP_ID, GRP_NAME) VALUES(27,"Unsecured Loans") INSERT INTO ACC_MASTER.DBO.GROUP_MASTER(GRP_ID, GRP_NAME) VALUES(28,"JobSales") INSERT INTO ACC_MASTER.DBO.GROUP_MASTER(GRP_ID, GRP_NAME) VALUES(29,"SalesReturn") INSERT INTO ACC_MASTER.DBO.GROUP_MASTER(GRP_ID, GRP_NAME) VALUES(30,"PurchaseReturn") INSERT INTO ACC_MASTER.DBO.GROUP_MASTER(GRP_ID, GRP_NAME) VALUES(31,"Creditors For Services") SET @SQL = "" SET @SQL = " INSERT INTO GROUP_MASTER(GRP_ID, /****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[PRO_FETCH_SALES_INVOICE_MASTER]    Script Date: 06/26/2026 15:55:51 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER OFF
GO
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[PRO_FETCH_SALES_INVOICE_MASTER] @Sal_Inv_Id_from as numeric, @Sal_Inv_Id_To as numeric, @cmp_code as int AS begin select si.*,lm.Lgr_Name as Party_Name,lm.Lgr_Add1 as Party_Add1,lm.Lgr_Add2 as Party_Add2, lcm.City_Name as Party_City_Name,lcm.City_PinCode as Party_City_PinCode, tm.Transport_Name,cm.City_Name as Station_Name, alm.Lgr_Name as Agent_Name, cmp.* from Sales_Invoice si left outer join Ledger_Master lm on si.Lgr_Id = lm.Lgr_Id left outer join Transport_Master tm on si.Transport_Id = tm.Transport_Id left outer join city_Master cm on si.Station_Id = cm.city_Id left outer join Ledger_Master alm on si.Agent_Id = alm.Lgr_Id left outer join city_Master lcm on lm.City_Id = lcm.City_Id left outer join Company_Master cmp on si.cmp_code = cmp.cmp_code where si.Sal_Inv_Id between @Sal_Inv_Id_from and @Sal_Inv_Id_To and si.cmp_code = 1 end RETURN
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[PRO_DELETE_MASTER_RECORDS]    Script Date: 06/26/2026 15:55:51 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER OFF

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[PRO_DELETE_MASTER_RECORDS] ( @ID AS NVARCHAR(10), @TABLE_NAME AS NVARCHAR(50), @CMP_CODE AS INT, @IS_DBDEFAULT AS NVARCHAR(1) ) AS BEGIN IF (@TABLE_NAME = "ITEM_MASTER") BEGIN DELETE FROM ITEM_MASTER WHERE ITEM_ID = @ID DELETE FROM ITEM_OPENING_STOCK WHERE ITEM_ID = @ID IF (@IS_DBDEFAULT = "1") BEGIN DELETE FROM ACC_MASTER.DBO.ITEM_MASTER WHERE ITEM_ID = @ID END END IF (@TABLE_NAME = "TRADE_MASTER") BEGIN DELETE FROM TRADE_MASTER WHERE TRADE_ID = @ID IF (@IS_DBDEFAULT = "1") BEGIN DELETE FROM ACC_MASTER.DBO.TRADE_MASTER WHERE TRADE_ID = @ID END END IF (@TABLE_NAME = "LOT_MASTER") BEGIN DELETE FROM LOT_MASTER WHERE LOT_ID = @ID IF (@IS_DBDEFAULT = "1") BEGIN DELETE FROM ACC_MASTER.DBO.LOT_MASTER WHERE LOT_ID = @ID END END IF (@TABLE_NAME = "PROCESS_MASTER") BEGIN DELETE FROM PROCESS_MASTER WHERE PROCESS_ID = @ID IF (@IS_DBDEFAULT = "1") BEGIN DELETE FROM ACC_MASTER.DBO.PROCESS_MASTER WHERE PROCESS_ID = @ID END END IF (@TABLE_NAME = "LORIWALA_MASTER") BEGIN DELETE FROM LORIWALA_MASTER WHERE LORIWALA_ID = @ID IF (@IS_DBDEFAULT = "1") BEGIN DELETE FROM ACC_MASTER.DBO.LORIWALA_MASTER WHERE LORIWALA_ID = @ID END END IF (@TABLE_NAME = "UNIT_MASTER") BEGIN DELETE FROM UNIT_MASTER WHERE UNIT_ID = @ID IF (@IS_DBDEFAULT = "1") BEGIN DELETE FROM ACC_MASTER.DBO.UNIT_MASTER WHERE UNIT_ID = @ID END END IF (@TABLE_NAME = "HASTE_MASTER") BEGIN DELETE FROM HASTE_MASTER WHERE HASTE_ID = @ID IF (@IS_DBDEFAULT = "1") BEGIN DELETE FROM ACC_MASTER.DBO.HASTE_MASTER WHERE HASTE_ID = @ID END END IF (@TABLE_NAME = "ITEM_GROUP_MASTER") BEGIN DELETE FROM ITEM_GROUP_MASTER WHERE ITEM_GRP_ID = @ID IF (@IS_DBDEFAULT = "1") BEGIN DELETE FROM ACC_MASTER.DBO.ITEM_GROUP_MASTER WHERE ITEM_GRP_ID = @ID END END IF (@TABLE_NAME = "CITY_MASTER") BEGIN DELETE FROM CITY_MASTER WHERE CITY_ID = @ID IF (@IS_DBDEFAULT = "1") BEGIN DELETE FROM ACC_MASTER.DBO.CITY_MASTER WHERE CITY_ID = @ID END END IF (@TABLE_NAME = "STATE_MASTER") BEGIN DELETE FROM STATE_MASTER WHERE STATE_ID = @ID IF (@IS_DBDEFAULT = "1") BEGIN DELETE FROM ACC_MASTER.DBO.STATE_MASTER WHERE STATE_ID = @ID END END IF (@TABLE_NAME = "GROUP_MASTER") BEGIN DELETE FROM GROUP_MASTER WHERE GRP_ID = @ID IF (@IS_DBDEFAULT = "1") BEGIN DELETE FROM ACC_MASTER.DBO.GROUP_MASTER WHERE GRP_ID = @ID END END IF (@TABLE_NAME = "TRANSPORT_MASTER") BEGIN DELETE FROM TRANSPORT_MASTER WHERE TRANSPORT_ID = @ID IF (@IS_DBDEFAULT = "1") BEGIN DELETE FROM ACC_MASTER.DBO.TRANSPORT_MASTER WHERE TRANSPORT_ID = @ID END END IF (@TABLE_NAME = "CATEGORY_MASTER") BEGIN DELETE FROM CATEGORY_MASTER WHERE CATEGORY_ID = @ID IF (@IS_DBDEFAULT = "1") BEGIN DELETE FROM ACC_MASTER.DBO.CATEGORY_MASTER WHERE CATEGORY_ID = @ID END END IF (@TABLE_NAME = "GENERAL_GROUP_MASTER") BEGIN DELETE FROM GENERAL_GROUP_MASTER WHERE GEN_GRP_ID = @ID IF (@IS_DBDEFAULT = "1") BEGIN DELETE FROM ACC_MASTER.DBO.GENERAL_GROUP_MASTER WHERE GEN_GRP_ID = @ID END END IF (@TABLE_NAME = "CUSTOMER_GROUP_MASTER") BEGIN DELETE FROM CUSTOMER_GROUP_MASTER WHERE CUST_GRP_ID = @ID IF (@IS_DBDEFAULT = "1") BEGIN DELETE FROM ACC_MASTER.DBO.CUSTOMER_GROUP_MASTER WHERE CUST_GRP_ID = @ID END END IF (@TABLE_NAME = "SUPPLIER_GROUP_MASTER") BEGIN DELETE FROM SUPPLIER_GROUP_MASTER WHERE SUPP_GRP_ID = @ID IF (@IS_DBDEFAULT = "1") BEGIN DELETE FROM ACC_MASTER.DBO.SUPPLIER_GROUP_MASTER WHERE SUPP_GRP_ID = @ID END END IF (@TABLE_NAME = "LEDGER_MASTER") BEGIN DELETE FROM LEDGER_DETAIL WHERE LGR_ID = @ID DELETE FROM LEDGER_MASTER WHERE LGR_ID = @ID IF (@IS_DBDEFAULT = "1") BEGIN DELETE FROM ACC_MASTER.DBO.LEDGER_MASTER WHERE LGR_ID = @ID END END IF (@TABLE_NAME = "WEAVER_MASTER") BEGIN DELETE FROM WEAVER_MASTER WHERE WEAVER_ID = @ID IF (@IS_DBDEFAULT = "1") BEGIN DELETE FROM ACC_MASTER.DBO.WEAVER_MASTER WHERE WEAVER_ID = @ID END END IF (@TABLE_NAME = "GODOWN_MASTER") BEGIN DELETE FROM GODOWN_MASTER WHERE GODOWN_ID= @ID IF (@IS_DBDEFAULT = "1") BEGIN DELETE FROM ACC_MASTER.DBO.GODOWN_MASTER WHERE GODOWN_ID = @ID END END IF (@TABLE_NAME = "DEDUCTEE_MASTER") BEGIN DELETE FROM DEDUCTEE_MASTER WHERE DEDUCTEE_CODE= @ID DELETE FROM DEDUCTEE_DETAIL WHERE DEDUCTEE_CODE = @ID END IF (@TABLE_NAME = "TDSNATURE") BEGIN DELETE FROM TDSNATURE WHERE TDSNATURE_CODE= @ID DELETE FROM TDSNATURE_DETAIL WHERE TDSNATURE_CODE = @ID END IF (@TABLE_NAME = "SCREEN_MASTER") BEGIN DELETE FROM SCREEN_MASTER WHERE SCREEN_ID= @ID IF (@IS_DBDEFAULT = "1") BEGIN DELETE FROM ACC_MASTER.DBO.SCREEN_MASTER WHERE SCREEN_ID = @ID END END IF (@TABLE_NAME = "SALESMAN_MASTER") BEGIN DELETE FROM SALESMAN_MASTER WHERE SALESMAN_ID= @ID IF (@IS_DBDEFAULT ="1") BEGIN DELETE FROM ACC_MASTER.DBO.SALESMAN_MASTER WHERE SALESMAN_ID = @ID END END IF (@TABLE_NAME = "MARKA_MASTER") BEGIN DELETE FROM MARKA_MASTER WHERE MARKA_ID= @ID IF (@IS_DBDEFAULT = "1") BEGIN DELETE FROM ACC_MASTER.DBO.MARKA_MASTER WHERE MARKA_ID = @ID END END IF (@TABLE_NAME = "CHART_MASTER") BEGIN DELETE FROM CHART_MASTER WHERE CHART_ID= @ID IF (@IS_DBDEFAULT = "1") BEGIN DELETE FROM ACC_MASTER.DBO.CHART_MASTER WHERE CHART_ID = @ID END END IF (@TABLE_NAME="CHEQUE_SERIES_MASTER") BEGIN DELETE FROM CHEQUE_SERIES_MASTER WHERE CHQ_SERIES_ID=@ID END IF (@TABLE_NAME="INSURANCE_MASTER") BEGIN DELETE FROM INSURANCE_MASTER WHERE INSURANCE_ID=@ID END IF (@TABLE_NAME = "SALES_INVOICE") BEGIN DELETE FROM SALES_INVOICE WHERE FLAG="S" AND SAL_INV_ID = @ID AND CMP_CODE = @CMP_CODE DELETE FROM SALES_INVOICE_DETAIL WHERE FLAG="S" AND SAL_INV_ID = @ID DELETE FROM PARTYDETAIL WHERE JOBFLAG="S" AND VCODE = @ID DELETE FROM TRANSPORT_DETAIL WHERE SAL_INV_ID = @ID DELETE FROM TRAN_DETAIL WHERE TRAN_ID = @ID AND CMP_CODE = @CMP_CODE AND TRAN_TYPE="S" DELETE FROM TRAN_MASTER WHERE TRAN_ID = @ID AND CMP_CODE = @CMP_CODE AND TRAN_TYPE="S" END IF (@TABLE_NAME = "SALES_ORDER") BEGIN DELETE FROM SALES_ORDER WHERE SAL_ORDER_ID = @ID DELETE FROM SALES_ORDER_DETAIL WHERE SAL_ORDER_ID = @ID DELETE FROM ASSORTMENT WHERE SAL_ORDER_ID = @ID DELETE FROM ASSORTMENT_DETAIL WHERE SAL_ORDER_ID = @ID END IF (@TABLE_NAME = "PACKINGSLIP") BEGIN DELETE FROM PACKINGSLIP WHERE PACKINGSLIPID = @ID DELETE FROM PACKINGSLIP_DETAIL WHERE PACKINGSLIPID = @ID DELETE FROM PACKINGSLIP_DETAILDETAIL WHERE PACKINGSLIPID = @ID DELETE FROM PACKINGSLIPDESIGN_DETAIL WHERE PACKINGSLIPID = @ID END IF (@TABLE_NAME = "COTTON_SALESINVOICE_MASTER") BEGIN DELETE FROM COTTON_SALESINVOICE_DETAIL WHERE COT_SAL_INV_ID = @ID AND CMP_CODE = @CMP_CODE DELETE FROM COTTON_SALESINVOICE_MASTER WHERE COT_SAL_INV_ID = @ID AND CMP_CODE = @CMP_CODE DELETE FROM TRAN_DETAIL WHERE TRAN_ID = @ID AND CMP_CODE = @CMP_CODE AND TRAN_TYPE="CA" DELETE FROM TRAN_MASTER WHERE TRAN_ID = @ID AND CMP_CODE = @CMP_CODE AND TRAN_TYPE="CA" END IF (@TABLE_NAME = "GREYPURCHASEORDER") BEGIN TDSENTRY_ID= @ID and Tran_Type='BP' DELETE FROM TRAN_DETAIL WHERE TDSENTRY_ID= @ID and Tran_Type='BP' END IF (@TABLE_NAME ="ExportBank_Master") BEGIN DELETE FROM ExportBank_Master WHERE Bank_Id=@ID IF (@IS_DBDEFAULT = "1") BEGIN DELETE FROM ACC_MASTER.DBO.ExportBank_Master WHERE Bank_Id = @ID END END IF (@TABLE_NAME = "PERFORMA_INVOICE_MASTER") BEGIN DELETE FROM PERFORMA_INVOICE_MASTER WHERE PER_INV_ID= @ID AND FLAG="PIM" DELETE FROM PERFORMA_INVOICE_DETAIL WHERE PER_INV_ID= @ID AND FLAG="PIM" END
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[INSERTQRCODE]    Script Date: 06/26/2026 15:55:51 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER OFF
GO
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[INSERTQRCODE] ( @IRN AS NVARCHAR(1500), @ACK_NO AS BIGINT, @ACK_DATE AS NVARCHAR(50), @IMAGE AS IMAGE, @BILLNO AS INT, @CMP_CODE AS INT, @TYPE AS NVARCHAR(20) ) AS IF @TYPE = "SALESINVOICE" BEGIN UPDATE SALES_INVOICE SET IRN= @IRN , EINVNO=@ACK_NO, ACK_DATE=@ACK_DATE, SIGNED_QR_CODE= @IMAGE WHERE SAL_INV_BILL_NO = @BILLNO AND CMP_CODE = @CMP_CODE END IF @TYPE = "JOBSALES" BEGIN UPDATE Job_SalesInvoice_Master SET IRN= @IRN , EINVNO=@ACK_NO, ACK_DATE=@ACK_DATE, SIGNED_QR_CODE= @IMAGE WHERE Job_Sal_Inv_Bill_No = @BILLNO AND CMP_CODE = @CMP_CODE END IF @TYPE = "SALESRETURN" BEGIN UPDATE SALES_RETURN_MASTER SET IRN= @IRN, EINVNO= @ACK_NO , ACK_DATE= @ACK_DATE, SIGNED_QR_CODE= @IMAGE WHERE DocNo = @BILLNO AND CMP_CODE = @CMP_CODE END IF @TYPE = "CREDITNOTE" BEGIN UPDATE CreditNoteAcc_Master SET IRN= @IRN, EINVNO=@ACK_NO, ACK_DATE=@ACK_DATE, SIGNED_QR_CODE= @IMAGE WHERE Tran_DocNo = @BILLNO AND CMP_CODE = @CMP_CODE END IF @TYPE = "DEBITNOTE" BEGIN UPDATE DebitNoteAcc_Master SET IRN= @IRN, EINVNO=@ACK_NO, ACK_DATE=@ACK_DATE, SIGNED_QR_CODE= @IMAGE WHERE Tran_DocNo= @BILLNO AND CMP_CODE = @CMP_CODE END IF @TYPE = "GRAYSALES" BEGIN UPDATE SALES_INVOICE SET IRN= @IRN , EINVNO=@ACK_NO, ACK_DATE=@ACK_DATE, SIGNED_QR_CODE= @IMAGE WHERE SAL_INV_BILL_NO = @BILLNO AND CMP_CODE = @CMP_CODE AND FLAG = 'GSN' END IF @TYPE = "MSALES" BEGIN UPDATE SALES_INVOICE SET IRN= @IRN , EINVNO=@ACK_NO, ACK_DATE=@ACK_DATE, SIGNED_QR_CODE= @IMAGE WHERE SAL_INV_BILL_NO = @BILLNO AND CMP_CODE = @CMP_CODE AND FLAG = 'MS' END
GO
/****** Object:  Default [DF_TRAN_MASTER_BRDOCNO]    Script Date: 06/26/2026 15:55:50 ******/
ALTER TABLE [dbo].[TRAN_MASTER] ADD  CONSTRAINT [DF_TRAN_MASTER_BRDOCNO]  DEFAULT ((0)) FOR [BRDOCNO]
GO
